the\n1081: // endpoint's program. Returns an error if the provided options are not valid,\n1082: // if there was an issue triggering policy updates for the given endpoint,\n1083: // or if endpoint regeneration was unable to be triggered. \t\t// No valid transitions, as disconnected and invalid are terminal\n1467: \t\t// states for the endpoint.\n1468: \tcase StateWaitingToRegenerate:\n1469: \t\tswitch toState {\n1470: \t\t// Note that transitions to StateWaitingToRegenerate are not allowed,\n1471: \t\t// as callers of this function enqueue regenerations if 'true' is\n1472: \t\t// returned. We don't want to return 'true' for the case of\n1473: \t\t// transitioning to StateWaitingToRegenerate, as this means that a\n1474: \t\t// regeneration is already queued up. Callers would then queue up\n1475: \t\t// another unneeded regeneration, which is undesired.\n1476: \t\t// Transition to StateWaitingForIdentity is also not allowed as that\n1477: \t\t// will break the ensuing regeneration.\n1478: \t\tcase StateDisconnecting, StateRestoring:\n1479: \t\t\tgoto OKState\n1480: \t\t// Don't log these state transition being invalid below so that we don't\n1481: \t\t// put warnings in the logs for a case which does not result in incorrect\n1482: \t\t// behavior.\n1483: \t\tcase StateWaitingForIdentity, StateWaitingToRegenerate:\n1484: \t\t\treturn false\n1485: \t\t}\n1486: \tcase StateRegenerating:\n1487: \t\tswitch toState {\n1488: \t\t// Even while the endpoint is regenerating it is\n1489: \t\t// possible that further changes require a new\n1490: \t\t// build. \t\te.getLogger().WithFields(logrus.Fields{\n1505: \t\t\tlogfields.EndpointState + \".from\": fromState,\n1506: \t\t\tlogfields.EndpointState + \".to\":   toState,\n1507: \t\t\t\"file\": BuilderSetStateLocked modifies the endpoint's state\n1534: // endpoint.mutex must be Lock()ed\n1535: // endpoint buildMutex must be held!\n1536: func (e *Endpoint) BuilderSetStateLocked(toState State, reason string) bool {\n1537: \t// Validate the state transition.\n1538: \tfromState := e.state\n1539: \tswitch fromState { // From state\n1540: \tcase StateWaitingForIdentity, StateReady, StateDisconnecting, StateDisconnected, StateInvalid:\n1541: \t\t// No valid transitions for the builder\n1542: \tcase StateWaitingToRegenerate, StateRestoring:\n1543: \t\tswitch toState {\n1544: \t\t// Builder transitions the endpoint from\n1545: \t\t// waiting-to-regenerate state to regenerating state\n1546: \t\t// right after acquiring the endpoint lock, and while\n1547: \t\t// endpoint's build mutex is held. All changes to\n1548: \t\t// cilium and endpoint configuration, policy as well\n1549: \t\t// as the existing set of security identities will be\n1550: \t\t// reconsidered after this point, i.e., even if some\n1551: \t\t// of them are changed regeneration need not be queued\n1552: \t\t// if the endpoint is already in waiting-to-regenerate\n1553: \t\t// state.\n1554: \t\tcase StateRegenerating:\n1555: \t\t\tgoto OKState\n1556: \t\t// Transition to ReadyState is not supported, but is\n1557: \t\t// attempted when a regeneration is competed, and another\n1558: \t\t// regeneration has been queued in the meanwhile. So this\n1559: \t\t// is expected and will not be logged as an error or warning.\n1560: \t\tcase StateReady:\n1561: \t\t\treturn false\n1562: \t\t}\n1563: \tcase StateRegenerating:\n1564: \t\tswitch toState {\n1565: \t\t// While still holding the build mutex, the builder\n1566: \t\t// tries to transition the endpoint to ready\n1567: \t\t// state. But since the endpoint mutex was released\n1568: \t\t// for the duration of the bpf generation, it is\n1569: \t\t// possible that another build request has been\n1570: \t\t// queued. In this case the endpoint has been\n1571: \t\t// transitioned to waiting-to-regenerate state\n1572: \t\t// already, and the transition to ready state is\n1573: \t\t// skipped (but not worth logging state transition to %s due to: %s\", toState, reason))\n1580: \treturn false\n1581: \n1582: OKState:\n1583: \te.state = toState\n1584: \te.logStatusLocked(Other, OK, reason)\n1585: \n1586: \tif states, after which\n1592: \t// the endpoint is gone or doesn't exist, we should not increment metrics\n1593: \t// for these states.\n1594: \tif toState != \"\" && toState != StateDisconnected && toState != StateInvalid {\n1595: \t\tmetrics.EndpointStateCount.\n1596: \t\t\tWithLabelValues(string(toState)).Inc()\n1597: \t}\n1598: \treturn true\n1599: }\n1600: \n1601: // OnProxyPolicyUpdate is a
